 mumbai ko apana aglaa match buudhvaar ko royal chalangers bangalore ke khilaaf khelnaa he

 ) Britain's Prime Minister David Cameron has assured Prime Minister Narendra Modi of Britain's strong support for India's effort for membership of the Nuclear Suppliers Group (NSG)
 yah kadam enesji kii agle saptaah hone vaali mahatvapurn baithak se pehle bharat ko majbootee pradaan karne vaala he
 Cameron on Thursday telephoned Modi to confirm Britain's support for India's membership in the 48-member NSG
 downing street ke ek pravaktaa ne kaha, ‘‘pradhanmantri ne bhartiya pradhanmantri narendra modi se parmaanu aapurtikarta samooh kii sadsyta ke liye bharat ke aavedan ke bare main baat kii
 This group of nuclear supplier countries works together to prevent nuclear proliferation by controlling the export of materials, equipment and technology that can be used to make nuclear weapons
 ’’ According to the spokesperson, "the Prime Minister confirmed that Britain would strongly support India's application
" unhone is baat par sahmati jataai ki prayaas ko safal banane ke liye bharat ke liye aprasar ke pramaanon ko majboot karte rahanaa mahatvapurn hoga jisamen asainya or sainya parmaanu gatividhiyon ke bich bhed karnaa shaamil he
 The two leaders also took stock of the uk-india relationship in a telephone conversation
 pravaktaa ne kaha ki unhone is baat ko mana ki britain-bharat sambandh majboot ho rahe hai jiske kaarnon main britain ke rajkumaar prince wiliam or unki patni cat kii haalia bharat yatra bhi shaamil he
 India's effort for membership of the NSG has also received a boost from the US, which has written to other members to support India's effort in the plenary session of the group to be held in Seoul on 24 June
 jahaan is pratishthit samooh main se adhiktar deshon ne bharat kii sadsyta kaa samarthan kiya he, vahiin china ke saath newjiland, ireland, turki, dakshin africa or austria isamen bharat ke pravesh ke pakshdhar nahin hai
 China is registering opposition to India's entry, arguing that it has not signed the Nuclear non-proliferation Treaty (NPT)
 china chahta he ki agar enesji bharat ko kisi tarah kii chhot detaa he to uske kareebi sahyogi pakistan ko bhi sadsyta pradaan kii jaae
 India is emphasizing that it is not necessary to sign the NPT to join the NSG
 bharat ne is babat france kaa udhaaharan dete hue kaha ki is tarah kii misaal pehle bhi dekhne ko mili he
 India is in touch with the member countries of the group to enter the NSG
 enesji aam-sahmati ke siddhant ke tahat kaam karata he or bharat ke khilaaf ek bhi desh kaa vot uske prayaas ko baadhit kar saktaa he

 camran ne guuruuvaar ko modi se phone par baatcheet kar 48 sadasyeey enesji main bharat kii sadsyta ke liye britain ke samarthan kii pushti kii
 a spokesperson for Downing Street said, "the Prime Minister talked to Indian Prime Minister Narendra Modi about India's application for membership of the Nuclear Suppliers Group
" parmaanu aapurtikarta deshon kaa yah samooh parmaanu hathiyaaron ko banane main istemaal ho sakane vaali saamagree, upkarnon or praudyogiki ke niryaat par niyantran karke parmaanu prasar ko rokane ke liye milakar kaam karata he
 '' pravaktaa ke anusaar, ‘‘pradhanmantri ne is baat kii pushti kii ki britain bharat ke aavedan kaa purajor samarthan karegaa
 He agreed that it would be important for India to continue to strengthen evidence of non-proliferation to make the effort a success, including a distinction between civilian and military nuclear activities
 ’’ donon netaaon ne telephone baatcheet main britain-bharat sambandhon kaa bhi jayja liya
 The spokesperson said that he recognized that uk-india relations were strengthening due to the recent visit of Prince William of Britain and his wife Kat to India
 enesji kii sadsyta ke liye bharat ke prayaas ko america se bhi bal mila he jisane anya sadasyon ko patr likhakar 24 june ko sol main yojit hone vaale samooh ke purna satr main bharat ke prayaas kaa samarthan karne ko kaha he
 While most of the countries in this prestigious group have supported India's membership, New Zealand, Ireland, Turkey, South Africa and Austria along with China are not in favor of India's entry into it
 china bharat ke pravesh par yah daleel dekar virodh darj kara rahaa he ki usne parmaanu aprasar sandhi (enpiti) par hastakshar nahin kiye hai
 China wants the membership to be extended to its close ally Pakistan if the NSG gives India some kind of leeway
 bharat is baat par jor de rahaa he ki enesji main shaamil hone ke liye enpiti par hastakshar karnaa jaruri nahin he
 India gave an example of France in this regard and said that such example has also been seen earlier
 bharat enesji main pravesh ke liye samooh ke sadsy deshon se sampark saadh rahaa he
 The NSG operates under the principle of consensus and a single country's vote against India can hamper its effort

 During the 38th day hearing in the Ayodhya case in the Supreme Court on Monday, advocate for Muslim parties Rajiv Dhawan told the court that the interesting thing is that during the hearing of this case all the questions are asked from us
 kabhi hindu paksh se sawaal nahin kiya jaataa
 Hindu parties objected to Dhawan's statement
 iske saath hi rajeev dhawan ne kaha ki hamane 6 disambar 1992 ko dhaancha giraae jane ke baad apni maang badali or hamaari yahi maang he ki hamen 5 disambar 1992 kii sthiti main jis tarah kaa dhaancha tha usee sthiti main hamen masjid saunpi jaae
 Dhawan said during the hearing of the case that i have not been given time to answer, the time limit fixed is not enough
 is maamle main bahut saare tathyon va kanoonee pahaluon ko court ke saamne rakhana he
 Both Rajiv Dhawan and CS Vaidyanathan, counsel for the Hindu parties, gave written arguments to the court
 dhawan ne kaha ki is baat ke koi saboot nahin die gaye kendriya gumbad ke neeche hi ram kaa janm hua
 No claim of Ram being born under the dome, offering flowers offerings to the devotees was proved
 gumbad ke neeche to trespassing kar log ghus aae the
 When worship was going on there, what does it mean to enter? This meant worship was being held outside
 kabhi bhi mandir todakar masjid nahin banaai
 There were frequent prayers
 dhawan ne kaha kiriti-rivaaj koi dimagi khel nahin he
 It cannot be mixed with confidence
 hindu paksh ne sabhi daleelon ko bina kisi tathyaatmak aadhaar or spashtikaran ke prastut kiya
 Hindus did not claim ownership of the land until 1989
 dhawan ne kaha ki 1885 or 1989 ke bich hindu paksh dwaara kabhi jameen ke tital kaa daawa nahin kiya gaya
 Whereas, from 1854 onwards, grants were given by the British Government for the maintenance of the Babri Masjid
 dhawan ne mana ki puratathvik sakshya ko pramanit kiya ja saktaa he
 However, earlier archeology was considered and rejected by Muslim parties as a social science
 dhawan ne kaha ki ASI report main kabhi ye nahin kaha gaya ki mandir ko todkar masjid banaai gai
 This place was always occupied by Muslims
 hinduon ne bahut baad main jameen ke tital kaa daawa kiya lekin use khaarij kar diya gaya
 He claimed adverse possession since 1934 for which there is no evidence
 saath hi unhone kaha ki yah dikhaane ke liye koi saboot nahin hai ki vaadi (hindu) vivaadit bhoomi kaa maalik he
 Hindus had only the right to use the land
 iske alaava koi adhikaar hinduon ko nahin diya gaya tha
 They were empowered to enter and pray through the eastern door, nothing more
 justise SA bobade or justise DY chandrachud ne kaha ki kya musalamaanon kaa ekmaatr adhikaar hone kaa daawa karnaa unki daleel ko halkaa nahin karegaa? jabaki hinduon ko bahari angan main pravesh karne kaa adhikaar tha
 Dhawan said that this does not give him rights
 justise DY chandrachud ne kaha ki kai dastauez he jo dikhaate he ki vah bahari angan main rahete the
 Dhawan said that he had no evidence to show that Hindu owns the disputed land of Babri Masjid
 ek bhi aisa dastavej nahin he jo sabit karata ho ki hinduon kaa vahaan par pehle kabza rahaa tha
 Justice DY Chandrachud asked Rajiv Dhawan about the occupation of the outer enclosure of the Hindus
 justise DY chandrachud ne kaha ki 1858 ke baad ke dastavejon se pataa chalata he ki ram chabutara kii sthapana kii gai thi, unke paas adhikaar tha
 Apart from this, Dhawan said that the Hindu side did not have any ownership document nor was it
 yah angrejon ke samay se vakf kii sampatti he or yahaan hinduon ne jabaran avaidh kabja kiya
 Hindus were given the right to worship and to be servants even though they did not have ownership
 1885-86 tak angrejon ne prarthana karne ke liye babari parisar ko hinduon ke liye purvi dwaar ko khol diya
 It was meant to maintain public order and nothing more
 vishwaas, yatra vrittant, skanda puraana unhen jameen kaa malikana haq nahin de sakate
 Possession of Muslims was never in doubt
 keval ek cheez jise tay karne kii aavashyaktaa he, vah unke bare main he
 He asked for permission to pray and now claimed his title
 centre sarkaar dwaara jammu evam kashmir samasya ke samaadhaan ke uddeshy se ghati main sabhi pakshon se baatcheet ke liye niyukt pratinidhi dineshwar sharma ne ajtak se khaas baatcheet main kaha he ki vah jald hi jammu kashmir jane vaale hai or unki koshish kashmir ko phir se swarg banane kii hogi
 Dineshwar Sharma said, "so far no terms have been given for talks by the government
 jaisaa ki grahamantri ne bataaya he or maine bhi saaf kiya he kii kashmir main jo bhi steke holder hai ham sabase baat karenge
 "he said," We are ready to talk the most, including the Hurriyat
 "algaavvaadiyon dwaara baatcheet karne se inkaar karne kii soochna dene par unhone kaha, "ham kashmir jane vaale hai or yah baatcheet ek yaa do din main puri hone vaali nahin he
 The problem is going to be this Sustain Dialogue in Kashmir
 hamaara uddeshy he ki kashmir main jald se jald shanti bahaali ho, sabhi log jammu kashmir main sukhi jivan bitaayen, bacchon kii padhai achche se chale, phir se kashmir swarg ban jaae
 "on the question of Kashmir youth adopting extremism, Dineshwar Sharma said that radicalization of youth in Kashmir is a big concern
 unhone kaha, "khud kashmir ke log is radicligeshan ko lekar sabase zyada chintit hai
 i sincerely hope that the people there are thinking about it and they will cooperate fully in it
 "kashmir main chalaae ja rahe online propeganda par unhone kaha kashmir ke yuvaaon ke bich ham ja rahe hai or mujhe lagata he ki kashmir ke yuva bahut samajhadaar hai, ve khud is baat ko samajhate hai or ikke dukke joonline propegandaamein shaamil hote hai, unako unke parivaar ke log hi samajhane main kaamyaab honge
 Dineshwar Sharma said that it is our wish and good luck that every youth of Kashmir should get employment and should get maximum work and all people should live in peace
 kashmir main aatankiyon ke khilaaf beete kuch samay se chalaae ja rahe vyapak saghan oparation ke maahaul main batcheet kii safalataa par sanshay vyakt karne par unhone kaha kaha, "kashmir main jo oparation chalaaya ja rahaa he vah diferent mudda he
 The operation that is being carried out is being conducted against the known terrorists
 ham to vahaan par aam janata se baatcheet karne ke liye ja rahe hai
 " garud parvamarch ke aakhri dinon membstar ke ped jab pattiyaan jhara chukte hai,dhoop tunakti he jangal jal uthta he
 In the night passing through a path, the fine flaring streak of fire moves like a snake in the midst of trees
 kya kisi ne barood bichaaya he? jameen ke neeche chuphi barudi khandak sulgi he? mandaraati maut? shuru dfa aisa hi lagata he
 Fire in Bastar is a decree of death
 bans kii ragad khaayi sukhi pattiyon se footati jangal main failati chingaari bhi kaartoos kaa nishaan detii he

 amarnath yatriyon par hamale ke baad kii raajnneeti upree str par kahin zyaada paripakv or sanbhalee hui he, lekin duusare darje ke netaaon, kaaryakartaaon or samarthakon ke bich is ghatana ko lekar pratikriyaayein sari simaaen paar kar gai hai
 We will come to that, but it is important to first look at some questions and aspects related to the incident
 bas driver shaikh saleem gafoor bhai ne samajhadaari na dikhaai hoti to aatankwaadi bas main savaar yatriyon par or kahar barapa sakate the
 Sheikh Salim lives in Raj apartment in Valsad, Gujarat and has been going to Amarnath for 8 years with passengers
 saleem ne bataaya ki aatankwaadi goliyaan chalaate rahe magar unhone bas roki nahin
 Bending his head, he just drove away at a speed of 70-80
 baahar ghanaa andhera tha or kuch nahin dikh rahaa tha

 usne ham sabaki jaan bachaa lee
 An hour after the incident, Salim Sheikh called his brother at nine thirty and told him everything
 jammu kashmir kii mukhyamantri mahabuuba mufti ne shaikh saleem ko 3 lakh rupee inaam dene kii ghoshnaa kii he
 Gujarat Chief Minister Vijay Rupani has said that he will write to the central government that Sheikh Salim should be given the medal of bravery
 bas kaa panjikaran hua tha yaa nahin
 From yesterday, news was coming from different sources that the bus is not registered with the Amarnath Shrine Board, otherwise it would have been crossed with Jawahar Tunnel with security guard at 12 noon
 saleem kaa kahana he ki bas kaa panjikaran hua tha varna yatri darshan kaise karte
 Visitation had already taken place on 2 July and travelers were doing tours
 hamaare sahyogi nazir ne apni report main likhaa he ki bas ne suraksha ke chah naake paar kiye magar use roka nahin gaya
 How can this happen, especially when there was a possibility of a terrorist attack any minute there
 saleem ne yah bhi bataaya ki uske saath kuch or basen bhi thim magar uski bas kaa tair panchar ho gaya to basen aage nikal gayi
 After recovering the puncture, Salim got ahead with his bus and got attacked
 raste main kuch jagahon par do teen suraksha karmchaaree dikhe magar sankhya kam thi isliye bas nahin roki
 Somewhere there is a statement that the darkness was so much that nothing was visible, somewhere the statement that if two or three security personnel were seen, the bus did not stop
 isliye lagata he ki saleem kaa bayaan mahatvapurn hote hue bhi yah chook kaise hui, use par aadhikarik or antim jawaab nahin mana janaa chahie
 The answer to this question is yet to be known as to whom the bus left Srinagar late in the evening
 kya yatriyon ne jor diya, kya yatriyon ko nahin pataa tha ki jokhim kaa kaam he
 Rajiv Ranjan says that the police of Jammu and Kashmir believe that the bus could not go on the highway after seven o'clock in the evening
 niyam hi nahin he to bas kaise gai or jab gai tab naake par kisi ne bas ko roka kyon nahin
 Even though Ram Madhav keeps defining the lapse, the Deputy Chief Minister also believes that there has been a lapse in security and should be investigated
 maharashtra ke dahanu se nirmala thakur bhi yatriyon main shaamil thim
 He died
 unki beti nitu singh ne yatra aayojak par laaparvaahee kaa aarope lagaaya he
 This incident has been opposed by all communities across the country, but many people on social media should also study separately the attempt to spread communal hysteria on the pretext of this incident
 ghatana ko lekar gussa or pratikriya kii aad main zimmedaar vyakti suraksha ko lekar sawaal nahin kar rahe the, kashmir kii nitiyon kii naakaami ko lekar sawaal nahin kar rahe the, un logon par sawaal kar rahe the jinka is ghatana se lenaa-dena nahin tha or jo purv kii hinsaatmak ghatnaon kii ninda karte rahe hai
 In the grip of this, a woman on the Twitter of Home Minister Rajnath Singh told him in vulgar language that who cares about Kashmiriyat
 aapkaa kaam tushtikaran nahin he
 Drag and fry those cowards
 to is par grahamantri ne chuppi nahin sadhi or na hi ghuma phiraa kar jawaab diya
 He said, Miss Kalra, it is my job to create peace and harmony in every part of the country, not all Kashmiri terrorists are
 public spes main rajnath singh kaa yah jawaab ek shandaar udhaaharan he
 He cared clearly about his constitutional responsibility, not caring about politics, that the job of the Home Minister is to worry and protect everyone
 unhone yah bhi kaha ki sabhi kashmiri aatankwaadi nahin hote hai
 Miss Kalra was also embarrassed in front of Rajnath Singh's decency and deleted her tweet
 iske liye miss kalra kii bhi tarif kii jaani chahie ki ve grahamantri kii baton ko samaj gayi
 Omar Abdullah also became convinced of Rajnath's reply and wrote that great Rajnathji, you have made me a muridar, i salute you
 aaj aapke netritv ke liye shukriya

 kaha he ki yah ghatana kashmiriat ke khilaaf he

 Someone began to hold intellectuals responsible for this, and some recently targeted Not in My Name demonstrations against mob violence
 note in maai nem ko kosa jane laga ki kya ab ve amarnath ke hindu yatriyon ke kilaaf pradarshan karenge
 There was a problem in front of such people, if they were going to protest themselves, they would have to shout slogans against the government of their choice, so they started targeting those who started demonstrating

 The way this campaign has been targeted, it seems that no protest will be considered as a protest until there will be a demonstration with the plank of Not in My Name
 yah unki badi kamyaabi he
 This game was being manipulated

 unhone kaha ki sansad sadsy ke rup main log hamen chunakar bhejte hai, unhen apekshaayen hoti he
 People hoped that something would be found in the railway budget but in the last two budgets you have disappointed them
 jan pratinidhi ke rup main hamen janata ko bataanaa hota he, isliye agle bajet main is baat kaa dhyaan rakhen
 Tapas Mandal of Trinamool Congress said that people were hopeful that Suresh Prabhu would give a new train, bring a new line, announce a new survey
 lekin aisa nahin hua
 The policy you have adopted may benefit in the future, but we are public representatives, we have to tell our people
 
 What do we tell them? Keep this in mind the next time you present the railway budget
 bhaajapa kii darshana jardosh ne kaha ki rail bajet main mantri ne pichhali pariyojnaon ko puraa karne par dhyaan diya, koi naye vaade nahin kiye balki lambit kaaryon ko puraa karne par jor diya
 It is welcome unhone kaha ki yatri suvidhaon evam swatchta ke vishay par vishesh dhyaan diya gaya he, saath hi soshal media ke jariye suresh prabhu yatriyon kii har sambhav madad karne kii pahal kar rahe hai
 He demanded a new train and train stoppage for his region Surat
 rakanpa ke tarik anwar ne kaha ki railway main badlaav laane kii ghoshnaaon ke baavjood samasyaayein barkaraar hai
 'these exercises are artificial and therefore remain problems
 ’’ unhone kaha ki sarkaar bullate train laana chaahati he, lekin aam log pareshaan hai
 Poor people go from one place to another for livelihood, they are financially weak, the Railway Minister should take care of their troubles
 ‘mek in india’ kaarykram kii aalochana karte hue rajd ke jaiprakash narayan yadav ne kaha ki railway main bhojan kii gunvattta or suraksha kii samasya bani hui he or railway ‘back in india’ ke rup main dikh rahaa he
 RP Maruthraja of AIADMK demanded to run a new train named 'amma Express'
 rail bajet kaa samarthan karte hue bhaajapa kii ranjanben bhatta ne kaha ki rail mantri ne bajet main railway evam yatri suvidhaon ko behatar banane kii disha main kai kadam uthaae hai
 He demanded a new train to connect Vadodara and Varanasi
 bhaajapa kii anju bala ne kaha ki bajet main maa, bacchon, varisht nagarikon samet sabhi virgon kii chintaaon kaa dhyaan rakhaa gaya he
 Praising the railway budget, bjp's Vinod Khanna said that all areas have been taken care of
 unhone rail kii raftaar ko badhaaye jane kii disha main pahal karne par dhyaan dene kii jarurat bataayi
 Former Prime Minister and Janata dal-sk HD Deve Gowda, while mentioning the announcement of 14 new railway lines in the Railway Budget for Karnataka during his Prime Ministership, said that those projects have not been completed till date
 unhone is baat ko sweekaar kiya ki rail mantri ke liye sansaadhan jutanaa ek badi chunauti he lekin aam aadmi ke liye yatra kaa sasta saadhan hone ke kaaran rail par logon kii aakankshaon kaa kaaphi dabaav rahata he
 Deve Gowda also attracted the attention of the Railway Minister to the fact that in the Southern Railway Division, trains are being run from very old coaches, causing inconvenience to the passengers
 bhaajapa kii bharti seya ne palitana or bandra ke bich saptaah main ek baar chalane vaali rail gaadi kaa istemaal saptaah ke baaki dinon main bhavnagar se dilli hote hue haridwar tak chalaae jane kii maang kii
 bjd's Prabhash Kumar Singh said that Odisha has been neglected for many years in the railway budget, but this time some justice has been done to it
 unhone iske saath hi 1882 main banaae gaye jharsuguda railway stesan ko railway divijan main tabdeel kiye jane kii maang kii
 The comments bhaajapa kii kamala devi patel ne rail bajet kii saraahna karte hue apane kshetra ke logon kii maangon ko rail mantri ke samaksh pesh kiya
 (this news has not been edited by the NDTV team
 yah syndicate feed se sidhe prakashit kii gai he) Former Minister of State for Railways and Congress member k h Muniyappa, while participating in the discussion on the Railway Budget for the year 2016-17, said that you have given a physical form budget while people had high expectations
 logon ko nai train, nai rail line, naye survey samet train tehraav evam anya ghoshnaaon kii apeksha thi lekin is bajet main aisa kuch nahin he
 He said that as members of Parliament, people elect and send us, they have expectations
 logon ko ummid thi ki rail bajet main kuch na kuch milegaa lekin pichley do bajet main aapane unhen niraash kiya he
 As a public representative, we have to tell the public, so keep this in mind in the next budget
 trinmul congress ke taapas mandal ne kaha ki logon ko ummid thi ki suresh prabhu nai train denge, nai line laaenge, nae survey kii ghoshnaa karenge
 but that did not happen
 aapane jo niti apanaai he, usase bhavishya main phayda ho saktaa he lekin ham janpratinidhi hai, hamen apane logon ko bataanaa hota he
 
 ham unhen kya bataaen? agali baar jab aap rail bajet pesh karen to iskaa dhyaan rakhen
 Darshana Zardosh of BJP said that in the Railway Budget, the minister focused on completing the previous projects, did not make any new promises but insisted on completing the pending works
 yah swaagatyogy he
 He said that special attention has been given to the subject of passenger amenities and cleanliness, as well as through social media, Suresh Prabhu is taking initiative to help travelers in every way possible
 unhone apane kshetra surat ke liye nai train or train tehraav kii maang kii
 ncp's Tariq Anwar said that despite the announcements to bring changes in the railways, the problems remain
 ‘ye kavayaden kritrim hai or isliye samasyaayein bani hui hai
 He said that the government wants to bring bullet train, but common people are upset
 garib log roji roti ke liye ek sthaan se duusare sthaan jate hai, ve aarthik rup se kamjor hote hai, rail mantri ko unki pareshaaniyon kaa dhyaan dena chahie
 Criticizing the 'make in India' program, rjd's Jayaprakash Narayan Yadav said that the quality and safety of food in the Railways remains a problem and the railway is showing as 'back in India'
 annadramuk ke aar pi marutharaja ne ‘ammaa express’ naam se nai train chalaane kii maang kii
 Supporting the rail budget, bjp's Ranjanben Bhatt said that the Railway Minister has taken several steps towards improving railway and passenger facilities in the budget
 unhone vadodara or varanasi ko jodne ke liye nai train kii maang kii
 bjp's Anju Bala said that the budget has taken care of the concerns of all sections including mother, children and senior citizens
 bhaajapa ke hi vinod khanna ne rail bajet kii prashansa karte hue kaha ki isamen sabhi kshetron kaa dhyaan rakhaa gaya he
 He stressed the need to focus on taking initiatives towards increasing the speed of the railways
 purv pradhanmantri or janata dal-es ke ech di devgauda ne unke pradhanmantritv kaal main karnataka ke liye rail bajet main 14 nai rail linon kii ghoshnaa kiye jane kaa ullekh karte hue kaha ki ve pariyojnaayen aaj tak bhi puri nahin hui hai
 He acknowledged that raising resources is a big challenge for the Railway Minister, but being a cheaper means of travel for the common man, there is a lot of pressure on people's aspirations on the railways
 devgauda ne is baat kii ore bhi rail mantri kaa dhyaan akshirt kiya ki dakshin railway mandal main trainon main kaaphi puraani bogiyon se kaam chalaaya ja rahaa he jisase yatriyon ko asuvidha kaa saamana karnaa padataa he
 bjp's Bharti Seya demanded that the train running between Palitana and Bandra once a week be used for the rest of the week from Bhavnagar to Delhi via Haridwar
 bijd ke prabhaash kumaar singh ne kaha ki odisha rail bajet main kaaphi saalon tak upekshit rahaa he lekin is baar uske saath kuch nyaay kiya gaya he
 He also demanded that the Jharsuguda railway station built in 1882 be converted into a railway division
 tippaniyan Kamla Devi Patel of BJP praised the Railway Budget and presented the demands of the people of her region to the Railway Minister
 (is khabar ko enditivi team ne sampadit nahin kiya he
